# Icons

Classes de ícones disponibilizadas para uso conforme os padrões do Liquid. .

# Uso do HTML
## Instuções de uso:


Sempre coloque a classe em e logo após a classe de algum ícone (prefixo sempre será icon-)
e complete com o resto do nome (variável): class="icon-[nome]"

```
<!-- O exemplo abaixo é do ícone lupa -->
<em class="icon-ui-search"></em>
Copy
```
## Como alterar cor e tamanho:

Usamos como referência o ícone [icon-accessibility-blind] - mas pode ser qualquer um disponibilizado no .

```
<em class="icon-accessibility-blind brad-text-color-cta-dark brad-icon-size-xs"></em>
Copy
```
## Valores possíveis para tamanho dos ícones:

| font-size | Valor |
| --- | --- |
| brad-icon-size-xxs | 16px |
| brad-icon-size-xs | 20px |
| brad-icon-size-sm | 24px |
| brad-icon-size-md | 32px |
| brad-icon-size-lg | 40px |
| brad-icon-size-xl | 48px |
| brad-icon-size-xxl | 56px |

# Exemplos


| Name | Description | Default | Control |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| theme | Altera segmento dos estilos string |  | Choose option... brad-theme-classic brad-theme-corporate brad-theme-empresas brad-theme-exclusive brad-theme-prime brad-theme-private brad-theme-next brad-theme-expresso brad-theme-classic-old brad-theme-exclusive-old brad-theme-prime-old brad-theme-private-old brad-theme-agora brad-theme-afluentes |
| textColor | Altera cor do texto string |  | Choose option... brad-text-color- brad-text-color-on-bg-primary brad-text-color-on-bg-secondary brad-text-color-primary brad-text-color-primary-light brad-text-color-primary-xlight brad-text-color-primary-dark brad-text-color-secondary brad-text-color-secondary-light brad-text-color-secondary-xlight brad-text-color-secondary-dark brad-text-color-institucional brad-text-color-institucional-light brad-text-color-institucional-xlight brad-text-color-institucional-dark brad-text-color-tertiary brad-text-color-cta brad-text-color-cta-light brad-text-color-cta-xlight brad-text-color-cta-dark brad-text-color-extended-green brad-text-color-extended-green-xlight brad-text-color-extended-green-dark brad-text-color-extended-blue brad-text-color-extended-blue-xlight brad-text-color-extended-blue-dark brad-text-color-extended-purple brad-text-color-extended-purple-xlight brad-text-color-extended-purple-dark brad-text-color-extended-violet brad-text-color-extended-violet-xlight brad-text-color-extended-violet-dark brad-text-color-extended-salmon brad-text-color-extended-salmon-xlight brad-text-color-extended-salmon-dark brad-text-color-extended-red brad-text-color-extended-red-xlight brad-text-color-extended-red-dark brad-text-color-extended-yellow brad-text-color-extended-yellow-xlight brad-text-color-extended-yellow-dark brad-text-color-alert-info brad-text-color-alert-info-light brad-text-color-alert-info-xlight brad-text-color-alert-info-dark brad-text-color-alert-success brad-text-color-alert-success-light brad-text-color-alert-success-xlight brad-text-color-alert-success-dark brad-text-color-alert-warning brad-text-color-alert-warning-light brad-text-color-alert-warning-xlight brad-text-color-alert-warning-dark brad-text-color-alert-error brad-text-color-alert-error-light brad-text-color-alert-error-xlight brad-text-color-alert-error-dark brad-text-color-neutral-100 brad-text-color-neutral-60 brad-text-color-neutral-50 brad-text-color-neutral-40 brad-text-color-neutral-30 brad-text-color-neutral-20 brad-text-color-neutral-10 brad-text-color-neutral-05 brad-text-color-neutral-0 |
| iconSize | Altera tamanho do ícone string |  | Choose option... brad-icon-size-xxs brad-icon-size-xs brad-icon-size-sm brad-icon-size-md brad-icon-size-lg brad-icon-size-xl brad-icon-size-xxl |
| icons | Filtre ícone pelo nome da classe string |  |  |
